        <h1 class="border-bottom-0">Apps</h1> 
        <div class="d-none d-lg-block ml-2"> <button class="btn-link Link--secondary js-print tooltipped tooltipped-n" aria-label="Print this article"> <!-- From https://heroicons.dev/ -->

       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div id="article-contents" class="article-grid-body"> 
       <p>The GitHub Apps API enables you to get high-level information about a GitHub App as well as specific information about installations of the app. To learn more about GitHub Apps, see "<a href="/en/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-a-github-app">Authenticating as a GitHub App</a>."</p> 
       <p>If you are using your app with GitHub Actions and want to modify workflow files, you must authenticate on behalf of the user with an OAuth token that includes the <code>workflow</code> scope. The user must have admin or write permission to the repository that contains the workflow file. For more information, see "<a href="/en/apps/building-oauth-apps/understanding-scopes-for-oauth-apps/#available-scopes">Understanding scopes for OAuth apps</a>."</p> 
       <p>This page lists endpoints that you can access while authenticated as a GitHub App. See "<a href="/en/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-a-github-app">Authenticating as a GitHub App</a>" to learn more.</p> 
       <p>When authenticated as a GitHub App, the GitHub Apps API enables you to get high-level information about a GitHub App as well as specific information about installations of an app.</p> 
       <p>You can access REST API v3 endpoints while authenticated as a GitHub App. These endpoints have a "Notes" section that contains a bullet point that says "Works with GitHub Apps." You can also access these endpoints while authenticated as a user.</p> 
       <p>A subset of REST API v3 endpoints requires authenticating as a GitHub App installation. See <a href="/en/rest/reference/apps#installations">Installations</a> for a list of these endpoints.</p> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="get-the-authenticated-app" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-the-authenticated-app">Get the authenticated app</a> </h3> 
         <p>Returns the GitHub App associated with the authentication credentials used. To see how many app installations are associated with this GitHub App, see the <code>installations_count</code> in the response. For more details about your app's installations, see the "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/apps#list-installations-for-the-authenticated-app">List installations for the authenticated app</a>" endpoint.</p> 
         <p>You must use a <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-a-github-app">JWT</a> to access this endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /app</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="get-the-authenticated-app--code-samples"> <a href="#get-the-authenticated-app--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/app</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'GET /app'</span>)
</code></pre> 
         <h4>Response</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 200 OK</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block">
          <pre><code class="hljs language-json">{

         <h4>Notes</h4> 
         <ul class="mt-2"> 
          <li><a href="/en/developers/apps">Works with GitHub Apps</a></li> 
         </ul> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="create-a-github-app-from-a-manifest" class="pt-3"> <a href="#create-a-github-app-from-a-manifest">Create a GitHub App from a manifest</a> </h3> 
         <p>Use this endpoint to complete the handshake necessary when implementing the <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/creating-github-apps-from-a-manifest/">GitHub App Manifest flow</a>. When you create a GitHub App with the manifest flow, you receive a temporary <code>code</code> used to retrieve the GitHub App's <code>id</code>, <code>pem</code> (private key), and <code>webhook_secret</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">post</span> /app-manifests/{code}/conversions</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="create-a-github-app-from-a-manifest--parameters"> <a href="#create-a-github-app-from-a-manifest--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>code</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="create-a-github-app-from-a-manifest--code-samples"> <a href="#create-a-github-app-from-a-manifest--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X POST \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/app-manifests/CODE/conversions</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'POST /app-manifests/{code}/conversions'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">code</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'code'</span>
})
</code></pre> 
         <h4>Response</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 201 Created</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block">
          <pre><code class="hljs language-json">{
  <span class="hljs-attr">"id"</span>: <span class="hljs-number">1</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"slug"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"octoapp"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"node_id"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"MDxOkludGVncmF0aW9uMQ=="</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"owner"</span>: {
    <span class="hljs-attr">"login"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"github"</span>,

         <h3 id="list-installations-for-the-authenticated-app" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-installations-for-the-authenticated-app">List installations for the authenticated app</a> </h3> 
         <p>You must use a <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-a-github-app">JWT</a> to access this endpoint.</p> 
         <p>The permissions the installation has are included under the <code>permissions</code> key.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /app/installations</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-installations-for-the-authenticated-app--parameters"> <a href="#list-installations-for-the-authenticated-app--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Results per page (max 100).</p> Default: <code>30</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Page number of the results to fetch.</p> Default: <code>1</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>since</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Only show notifications updated after the given time. This is a timestamp in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_8601">ISO 8601</a> format: <code>YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SSZ</code>.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>outdated</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="get-an-installation-for-the-authenticated-app" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-an-installation-for-the-authenticated-app">Get an installation for the authenticated app</a> </h3> 
         <p>Enables an authenticated GitHub App to find an installation's information using the installation id. The installation's account type (<code>target_type</code>) will be either an organization or a user account, depending which account the repository belongs to.</p> 
         <p>You must use a <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-a-github-app">JWT</a> to access this endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /app/installations/{installation_id}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="get-an-installation-for-the-authenticated-app--parameters"> <a href="#get-an-installation-for-the-authenticated-app--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>installation_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>installation_id parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="get-an-installation-for-the-authenticated-app--code-samples"> <a href="#get-an-installation-for-the-authenticated-app--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/app/installations/42</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'GET /app/installations/{installation_id}'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">installation_id</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>
})
</code></pre>

         <h3 id="delete-an-installation-for-the-authenticated-app" class="pt-3"> <a href="#delete-an-installation-for-the-authenticated-app">Delete an installation for the authenticated app</a> </h3> 
         <p>Uninstalls a GitHub App on a user, organization, or business account. If you prefer to temporarily suspend an app's access to your account's resources, then we recommend the "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/apps/#suspend-an-app-installation">Suspend an app installation</a>" endpoint.</p> 
         <p>You must use a <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-a-github-app">JWT</a> to access this endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /app/installations/{installation_id}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="delete-an-installation-for-the-authenticated-app--parameters"> <a href="#delete-an-installation-for-the-authenticated-app--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>installation_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>installation_id parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="delete-an-installation-for-the-authenticated-app--code-samples"> <a href="#delete-an-installation-for-the-authenticated-app--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X DELETE \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/app/installations/42</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'DELETE /app/installations/{installation_id}'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">installation_id</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>
})
</code></pre> 
         <h4>Response</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 204 No Content</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Resource not found</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 404 Not Found</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
        </div>

       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="create-an-installation-access-token-for-an-app" class="pt-3"> <a href="#create-an-installation-access-token-for-an-app">Create an installation access token for an app</a> </h3> 
         <p>Creates an installation access token that enables a GitHub App to make authenticated API requests for the app's installation on an organization or individual account. Installation tokens expire one hour from the time you create them. Using an expired token produces a status code of <code>401 - Unauthorized</code>, and requires creating a new installation token. By default the installation token has access to all repositories that the installation can access. To restrict the access to specific repositories, you can provide the <code>repository_ids</code> when creating the token. When you omit <code>repository_ids</code>, the response does not contain the <code>repositories</code> key.</p> 
         <p>You must use a <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-a-github-app">JWT</a> to access this endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">post</span> /app/installations/{installation_id}/access_tokens</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="create-an-installation-access-token-for-an-app--parameters"> <a href="#create-an-installation-access-token-for-an-app--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>installation_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>installation_id parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repositories</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array of strings</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>List of repository names that the token should have access to</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repository_ids</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array of integers</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>List of repository IDs that the token should have access to</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>permissions</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">object</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The permissions granted to the user-to-server access token.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr style="border: none;"> 
            <td colspan="4" class="has-nested-table">

                <tr>

                 <td class="opacity-60"><code>administration</code> (string)</td>

                <tr> 
                 <td class="opacity-60"><code>checks</code> (string)</td>

                </tr>

  ]

       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="suspend-an-app-installation" class="pt-3"> <a href="#suspend-an-app-installation">Suspend an app installation</a> </h3> 
         <p>Suspends a GitHub App on a user, organization, or business account, which blocks the app from accessing the account's resources. When a GitHub App is suspended, the app's access to the GitHub API or webhook events is blocked for that account.</p> 
         <p>You must use a <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-a-github-app">JWT</a> to access this endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">put</span> /app/installations/{installation_id}/suspended</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="suspend-an-app-installation--parameters"> <a href="#suspend-an-app-installation--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>installation_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>installation_id parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="suspend-an-app-installation--code-samples"> <a href="#suspend-an-app-installation--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X PUT \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/app/installations/42/suspended</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'PUT /app/installations/{installation_id}/suspended'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">installation_id</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>
})
</code></pre> 
         <h4>Response</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 204 No Content</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div>

         <h3 id="unsuspend-an-app-installation" class="pt-3"> <a href="#unsuspend-an-app-installation">Unsuspend an app installation</a> </h3> 
         <p>Removes a GitHub App installation suspension.</p> 
         <p>You must use a <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-a-github-app">JWT</a> to access this endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /app/installations/{installation_id}/suspended</code></pre> 
        <div>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="get-an-app" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-an-app">Get an app</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Note</strong>: The <code>:app_slug</code> is just the URL-friendly name of your GitHub App. You can find this on the settings page for your GitHub App (e.g., <code>https://github.com/settings/apps/:app_slug</code>).</p> 
         <p>If the GitHub App you specify is public, you can access this endpoint without authenticating. If the GitHub App you specify is private, you must authenticate with a <a href="https://help.github.com/articles/creating-a-personal-access-token-for-the-command-line/">personal access token</a> or an <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-an-installation">installation access token</a> to access this endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /apps/{app_slug}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="get-an-app--parameters"> <a href="#get-an-app--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4>

            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td>

           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>app_slug</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody>

         <h3 id="get-an-organization-installation-for-the-authenticated-app" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-an-organization-installation-for-the-authenticated-app">Get an organization installation for the authenticated app</a> </h3>

         <h3 id="get-a-repository-installation-for-the-authenticated-app" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-a-repository-installation-for-the-authenticated-app">Get a repository installation for the authenticated app</a> </h3> 
         <p>Enables an authenticated GitHub App to find the repository's installation information. The installation's account type will be either an organization or a user account, depending which account the repository belongs to.</p> 
         <p>You must use a <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-a-github-app">JWT</a> to access this endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/installation</code></pre>

       </div> 
       <h2 id="oauth-applications-api"><a href="#oauth-applications-api">OAuth Applications API</a></h2> 
       <p>You can use this API to manage the OAuth tokens an OAuth application uses to access people's GitHub accounts.</p> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="delete-an-app-authorization" class="pt-3"> <a href="#delete-an-app-authorization">Delete an app authorization</a> </h3> 
         <p>OAuth application owners can revoke a grant for their OAuth application and a specific user. You must use <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/other-authentication-methods#basic-authentication">Basic Authentication</a> when accessing this endpoint, using the OAuth application's <code>client_id</code> and <code>client_secret</code> as the username and password. You must also provide a valid OAuth <code>access_token</code> as an input parameter and the grant for the token's owner will be deleted. Deleting an OAuth application's grant will also delete all OAuth tokens associated with the application for the user. Once deleted, the application will have no access to the user's account and will no longer be listed on <a href="https://github.com/settings/applications#authorized">the application authorizations settings screen within GitHub</a>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /applications/{client_id}/grant</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="delete-an-app-authorization--parameters"> <a href="#delete-an-app-authorization--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>client_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The client ID of your GitHub app.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>access_token</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The OAuth access token used to authenticate to the GitHub API.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="delete-an-app-authorization--code-samples"> <a href="#delete-an-app-authorization--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X DELETE \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/applications/CLIENT_ID/grant \
  -d '{"access_token":"access_token"}'</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'DELETE /applications/{client_id}/grant'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">client_id</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'client_id'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">access_token</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'access_token'</span>
})
</code></pre> 
         <h4>Response</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 204 No Content</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Validation failed</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 422 Unprocessable Entity</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="revoke-a-grant-for-an-application" class="pt-3"> <a href="#revoke-a-grant-for-an-application">Revoke a grant for an application</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> GitHub will discontinue OAuth endpoints that contain <code>access_token</code> in the path parameter. We have introduced new endpoints that allow you to securely manage tokens for OAuth Apps by moving <code>access_token</code> to the request body. For more information, see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2020-02-14-deprecating-oauth-app-endpoint/">blog post</a>.</p> 
         <p>OAuth application owners can revoke a grant for their OAuth application and a specific user. You must use <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/other-authentication-methods#basic-authentication">Basic Authentication</a> when accessing this endpoint, using the OAuth application's <code>client_id</code> and <code>client_secret</code> as the username and password. You must also provide a valid token as <code>:access_token</code> and the grant for the token's owner will be deleted.</p> 
         <p>Deleting an OAuth application's grant will also delete all OAuth tokens associated with the application for the user. Once deleted, the application will have no access to the user's account and will no longer be listed on <a href="https://github.com/settings/applications#authorized">the Applications settings page under "Authorized OAuth Apps" on GitHub</a>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /applications/{client_id}/grants/{access_token}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="revoke-a-grant-for-an-application--parameters"> <a href="#revoke-a-grant-for-an-application--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented

        <div> 
         <h3 id="check-a-token" class="pt-3"> <a href="#check-a-token">Check a token</a> </h3> 
         <p>OAuth applications can use a special API method for checking OAuth token validity without exceeding the normal rate limits for failed login attempts. Authentication works differently with this particular endpoint. You must use <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/other-authentication-methods#basic-authentication">Basic Authentication</a> to use this endpoint, where the username is the OAuth application <code>client_id</code> and the password is its <code>client_secret</code>. Invalid tokens will return <code>404 NOT FOUND</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">post</span> /applications/{client_id}/token</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="check-a-token--parameters"> <a href="#check-a-token--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>client_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The client ID of your GitHub app.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>access_token</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Required</strong>. The access_token of the OAuth application.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="reset-a-token" class="pt-3"> <a href="#reset-a-token">Reset a token</a> </h3> 
         <p>OAuth applications can use this API method to reset a valid OAuth token without end-user involvement. Applications must save the "token" property in the response because changes take effect immediately. You must use <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/other-authentication-methods#basic-authentication">Basic Authentication</a> when accessing this endpoint, using the OAuth application's <code>client_id</code> and <code>client_secret</code> as the username and password. Invalid tokens will return <code>404 NOT FOUND</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">patch</span> /applications/{client_id}/token</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="reset-a-token--parameters"> <a href="#reset-a-token--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead>

            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>client_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The client ID of your GitHub app.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>access_token</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td>

         <h3 id="delete-an-app-token" class="pt-3"> <a href="#delete-an-app-token">Delete an app token</a> </h3> 
         <p>OAuth application owners can revoke a single token for an OAuth application. You must use <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/other-authentication-methods#basic-authentication">Basic Authentication</a> when accessing this endpoint, using the OAuth application's <code>client_id</code> and <code>client_secret</code> as the username and password.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /applications/{client_id}/token</code></pre>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="create-a-scoped-access-token" class="pt-3"> <a href="#create-a-scoped-access-token">Create a scoped access token</a> </h3> 
         <p>Use a non-scoped user-to-server OAuth access token to create a repository scoped and/or permission scoped user-to-server OAuth access token. You can specify which repositories the token can access and which permissions are granted to the token. You must use <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/other-authentication-methods#basic-authentication">Basic Authentication</a> when accessing this endpoint, using the OAuth application's <code>client_id</code> and <code>client_secret</code> as the username and password. Invalid tokens will return <code>404 NOT FOUND</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">post</span> /applications/{client_id}/token/scoped</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="create-a-scoped-access-token--parameters"> <a href="#create-a-scoped-access-token--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>client_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The client ID of your GitHub app.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>access_token</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Required</strong>. The OAuth access token used to authenticate to the GitHub API.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>target</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The name of the user or organization to scope the user-to-server access token to. <strong>Required</strong> unless <code>target_id</code> is specified.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>target_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The ID of the user or organization to scope the user-to-server access token to. <strong>Required</strong> unless <code>target</code> is specified.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repositories</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array of strings</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The list of repository names to scope the user-to-server access token to. <code>repositories</code> may not be specified if <code>repository_ids</code> is specified.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repository_ids</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array of integers</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The list of repository IDs to scope the user-to-server access token to. <code>repository_ids</code> may not be specified if <code>repositories</code> is specified.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>permissions</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">object</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The permissions granted to the user-to-server access token.</p> </td> 
           </tr>

         <h4 id="create-a-scoped-access-token--code-samples"> <a href="#create-a-scoped-access-token--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X POST \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/applications/CLIENT_ID/token/scoped \
  -d '{"access_token":"access_token"}'</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5>

  <span class="hljs-attr">access_token</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'access_token'</span>
})
</code></pre>

         <h4>Requires authentication</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 401 Unauthorized</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Forbidden</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 403 Forbidden</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Resource not found</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 404 Not Found</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Validation failed</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 422 Unprocessable Entity</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
        </div>

       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="check-an-authorization" class="pt-3"> <a href="#check-an-authorization">Check an authorization</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> GitHub will discontinue OAuth endpoints that contain <code>access_token</code> in the path parameter. We have introduced new endpoints that allow you to securely manage tokens for OAuth Apps by moving <code>access_token</code> to the request body. For more information, see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2020-02-14-deprecating-oauth-app-endpoint/">blog post</a>.</p> 
         <p>OAuth applications can use a special API method for checking OAuth token validity without exceeding the normal rate limits for failed login attempts. Authentication works differently with this particular endpoint. You must use <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/other-authentication-methods#basic-authentication">Basic Authentication</a> when accessing this endpoint, using the OAuth application's <code>client_id</code> and <code>client_secret</code> as the username and password. Invalid tokens will return <code>404 NOT FOUND</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /applications/{client_id}/tokens/{access_token}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="check-an-authorization--parameters"> <a href="#check-an-authorization--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>client_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The client ID of your GitHub app.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>access_token</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="reset-an-authorization" class="pt-3"> <a href="#reset-an-authorization">Reset an authorization</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> GitHub will discontinue OAuth endpoints that contain <code>access_token</code> in the path parameter. We have introduced new endpoints that allow you to securely manage tokens for OAuth Apps by moving <code>access_token</code> to the request body. For more information, see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2020-02-14-deprecating-oauth-app-endpoint/">blog post</a>.</p> 
         <p>OAuth applications can use this API method to reset a valid OAuth token without end-user involvement. Applications must save the "token" property in the response because changes take effect immediately. You must use <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/other-authentication-methods#basic-authentication">Basic Authentication</a> when accessing this endpoint, using the OAuth application's <code>client_id</code> and <code>client_secret</code> as the username and password. Invalid tokens will return <code>404 NOT FOUND</code>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">post</span> /applications/{client_id}/tokens/{access_token}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="reset-an-authorization--parameters"> <a href="#reset-an-authorization--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>client_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The client ID of your GitHub app.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>access_token</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="revoke-an-authorization-for-an-application" class="pt-3"> <a href="#revoke-an-authorization-for-an-application">Revoke an authorization for an application</a> </h3> 
         <p><strong>Deprecation Notice:</strong> GitHub will discontinue OAuth endpoints that contain <code>access_token</code> in the path parameter. We have introduced new endpoints that allow you to securely manage tokens for OAuth Apps by moving <code>access_token</code> to the request body. For more information, see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2020-02-14-deprecating-oauth-app-endpoint/">blog post</a>.</p> 
         <p>OAuth application owners can revoke a single token for an OAuth application. You must use <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/other-authentication-methods#basic-authentication">Basic Authentication</a> when accessing this endpoint, using the OAuth application's <code>client_id</code> and <code>client_secret</code> as the username and password.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /applications/{client_id}/tokens/{access_token}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="revoke-an-authorization-for-an-application--parameters"> <a href="#revoke-an-authorization-for-an-application--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead>

            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>client_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The client ID of your GitHub app.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>access_token</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

       <h2 id="installations"><a href="#installations">Installations</a></h2> 
       <p>The Installations API enables you to get information about installations of your GitHub App and perform actions within those installations. An <em>installation</em> refers to any user or organization account that has installed the app. For information on how to authenticate as an installation and limit access to specific repositories, see "<a href="/en/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-an-installation">Authenticating as an installation</a>."</p> 
       <p>To list all GitHub App installations for an organization, see "<a href="/en/rest/reference/orgs#list-app-installations-for-an-organization">List app installations for an organization</a>."</p> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-repositories-accessible-to-the-app-installation" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-repositories-accessible-to-the-app-installation">List repositories accessible to the app installation</a> </h3> 
         <p>List repositories that an app installation can access.</p> 
         <p>You must use an <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-an-installation">installation access token</a> to access this endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /installation/repositories</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-repositories-accessible-to-the-app-installation--parameters"> <a href="#list-repositories-accessible-to-the-app-installation--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. <a href="#list-repositories-accessible-to-the-app-installation-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Results per page (max 100).</p> Default: <code>30</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Page number of the results to fetch.</p> Default: <code>1</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

         <h4 id="list-repositories-accessible-to-the-app-installation-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>The <code>topics</code> property for repositories on GitHub is currently available for developers to preview. To view the <code>topics</code> property in calls that return repository results, you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.mercy-preview+json</code></pre>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="revoke-an-installation-access-token" class="pt-3"> <a href="#revoke-an-installation-access-token">Revoke an installation access token</a> </h3> 
         <p>Revokes the installation token you're using to authenticate as an installation and access this endpoint.</p> 
         <p>Once an installation token is revoked, the token is invalidated and cannot be used. Other endpoints that require the revoked installation token must have a new installation token to work. You can create a new token using the "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/apps#create-an-installation-access-token-for-an-app">Create an installation access token for an app</a>" endpoint.</p> 
         <p>You must use an <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-an-installation">installation access token</a> to access this endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /installation/token</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="revoke-an-installation-access-token--code-samples"> <a href="#revoke-an-installation-access-token--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X DELETE \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/installation/token</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'DELETE /installation/token'</span>)
</code></pre> 
         <h4>Response</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 204 No Content</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Notes</h4> 
         <ul class="mt-2"> 
          <li><a href="/en/developers/apps">Works with GitHub Apps</a></li> 
         </ul> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="create-a-content-attachment" class="pt-3"> <a href="#create-a-content-attachment">Create a content attachment</a> </h3> 
         <p>Creates an attachment under a content reference URL in the body or comment of an issue or pull request. Use the <code>id</code> and <code>repository</code> <code>full_name</code> of the content reference from the <a href="https://docs.github.com/webhooks/event-payloads/#content_reference"><code>content_reference</code> event</a> to create an attachment.</p> 
         <p>The app must create a content attachment within six hours of the content reference URL being posted. See "<a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/using-content-attachments/">Using content attachments</a>" for details about content attachments.</p> 
         <p>You must use an <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-an-installation">installation access token</a> to access this endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">post</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/content_references/{content_reference_id}/attachments</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="create-a-content-attachment--parameters"> <a href="#create-a-content-attachment--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> This API is under preview and subject to change. <a href="#create-a-content-attachment-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The owner of the repository. Determined from the <code>repository</code> <code>full_name</code> of the <code>content_reference</code> event.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The name of the repository. Determined from the <code>repository</code> <code>full_name</code> of the <code>content_reference</code> event.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>content_reference_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The <code>id</code> of the <code>content_reference</code> event.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>title</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Required</strong>. The title of the attachment</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>body</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Required</strong>. The body of the attachment</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="create-a-content-attachment--code-samples"> <a href="#create-a-content-attachment--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X POST \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.corsair-preview+json" \
  https://api.github.com/repos/octocat/hello-world/content_references/42/attachments \
  -d '{"title":"title","body":"body"}'</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'POST /repos/{owner}/{repo}/content_references/{content_reference_id}/attachments'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">owner</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'octocat'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">repo</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'hello-world'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">content_reference_id</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">title</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'title'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">body</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'body'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">mediaType</span>: {
    <span class="hljs-attr">previews</span>: [
      <span class="hljs-string">'corsair'</span>
    ]
  }
})
</code></pre> 
         <h4>Response</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 200 OK</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block">
          <pre><code class="hljs language-json">{
  <span class="hljs-attr">"id"</span>: <span class="hljs-number">101</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"title"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"[A-1234] Error found in core/models.py file'"</span>,

         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>To access the Content Attachments API during the preview period, you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.corsair-preview+json</code></pre> ?? This header is <strong>required</strong>.

        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-app-installations-accessible-to-the-user-access-token" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-app-installations-accessible-to-the-user-access-token">List app installations accessible to the user access token</a> </h3> 
         <p>Lists installations of your GitHub App that the authenticated user has explicit permission (<code>:read</code>, <code>:write</code>, or <code>:admin</code>) to access.</p> 
         <p>You must use a <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/identifying-and-authorizing-users-for-github-apps/#identifying-users-on-your-site">user-to-server OAuth access token</a>, created for a user who has authorized your GitHub App, to access this endpoint.</p> 
         <p>The authenticated user has explicit permission to access repositories they own, repositories where they are a collaborator, and repositories that they can access through an organization membership.</p> 
         <p>You can find the permissions for the installation under the <code>permissions</code> key.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /user/installations</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-app-installations-accessible-to-the-user-access-token--parameters"> <a href="#list-app-installations-accessible-to-the-user-access-token--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Results per page (max 100).</p> Default: <code>30</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Page number of the results to fetch.</p> Default: <code>1</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-repositories-accessible-to-the-user-access-token" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-repositories-accessible-to-the-user-access-token">List repositories accessible to the user access token</a> </h3> 
         <p>List repositories that the authenticated user has explicit permission (<code>:read</code>, <code>:write</code>, or <code>:admin</code>) to access for an installation.</p> 
         <p>The authenticated user has explicit permission to access repositories they own, repositories where they are a collaborator, and repositories that they can access through an organization membership.</p> 
         <p>You must use a <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/identifying-and-authorizing-users-for-github-apps/#identifying-users-on-your-site">user-to-server OAuth access token</a>, created for a user who has authorized your GitHub App, to access this endpoint.</p> 
         <p>The access the user has to each repository is included in the hash under the <code>permissions</code> key.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /user/installations/{installation_id}/repositories</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-repositories-accessible-to-the-user-access-token--parameters"> <a href="#list-repositories-accessible-to-the-user-access-token--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. <a href="#list-repositories-accessible-to-the-user-access-token-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>installation_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>installation_id parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Results per page (max 100).</p> Default: <code>30</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Page number of the results to fetch.</p> Default: <code>1</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

  <span class="hljs-attr">installation_id</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>
})
</code></pre>

         <h4 id="list-repositories-accessible-to-the-user-access-token-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>The <code>topics</code> property for repositories on GitHub is currently available for developers to preview. To view the <code>topics</code> property in calls that return repository results, you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.mercy-preview+json</code></pre> 
         </div> 
        </div>

       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="add-a-repository-to-an-app-installation" class="pt-3"> <a href="#add-a-repository-to-an-app-installation">Add a repository to an app installation</a> </h3> 
         <p>Add a single repository to an installation. The authenticated user must have admin access to the repository.</p> 
         <p>You must use a personal access token (which you can create via the <a href="https://docs.github.com/github/authenticating-to-github/creating-a-personal-access-token">command line</a> or <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/other-authentication-methods#basic-authentication">Basic Authentication</a>) to access this endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">put</span> /user/installations/{installation_id}/repositories/{repository_id}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="add-a-repository-to-an-app-installation--parameters"> <a href="#add-a-repository-to-an-app-installation--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead>

         <h3 id="remove-a-repository-from-an-app-installation" class="pt-3"> <a href="#remove-a-repository-from-an-app-installation">Remove a repository from an app installation</a> </h3> 
         <p>Remove a single repository from an installation. The authenticated user must have admin access to the repository.</p> 
         <p>You must use a personal access token (which you can create via the <a href="https://docs.github.com/github/authenticating-to-github/creating-a-personal-access-token">command line</a> or <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/other-authentication-methods#basic-authentication">Basic Authentication</a>) to access this endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /user/installations/{installation_id}/repositories/{repository_id}</code></pre>

       <h2 id="marketplace"><a href="#marketplace">Marketplace</a></h2> 
       <p>For more information about GitHub Marketplace, see "<a href="/en/marketplace">GitHub Marketplace</a>."</p> 
       <p>The GitHub Marketplace API allows you to see which customers are using a pricing plan, see a customer's purchases, and see if an account has an active subscription.</p> 
       <h3 id="testing-with-stubbed-endpoints"><a href="#testing-with-stubbed-endpoints">Testing with stubbed endpoints</a></h3> 
       <p>This API includes endpoints that allow you to <a href="/en/marketplace/integrating-with-the-github-marketplace-api/testing-github-marketplace-apps">test your GitHub App</a> with <strong>stubbed data</strong>. Stubbed data is hard-coded, fake data that will not change based on actual subscriptions.</p> 
       <p>To test with stubbed data, use a stubbed endpoint in place of its production counterpart. This allows you to test whether API logic succeeds before listing GitHub Apps on GitHub Marketplace.</p> 
       <p>Be sure to replace stubbed endpoints with production endpoints before deploying your GitHub App.</p> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="get-a-subscription-plan-for-an-account" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-a-subscription-plan-for-an-account">Get a subscription plan for an account</a> </h3> 
         <p>Shows whether the user or organization account actively subscribes to a plan listed by the authenticated GitHub App. When someone submits a plan change that won't be processed until the end of their billing cycle, you will also see the upcoming pending change.</p> 
         <p>GitHub Apps must use a <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-a-github-app">JWT</a> to access this endpoint. OAuth Apps must use <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/other-authentication-methods#basic-authentication">basic authentication</a> with their client ID and client secret to access this endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /marketplace_listing/accounts/{account_id}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="get-a-subscription-plan-for-an-account--parameters"> <a href="#get-a-subscription-plan-for-an-account--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-accounts-for-a-plan" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-accounts-for-a-plan">List accounts for a plan</a> </h3> 
         <p>Returns user and organization accounts associated with the specified plan, including free plans. For per-seat pricing, you see the list of accounts that have purchased the plan, including the number of seats purchased. When someone submits a plan change that won't be processed until the end of their billing cycle, you will also see the upcoming pending change.</p> 
         <p>GitHub Apps must use a <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-a-github-app">JWT</a> to access this endpoint. OAuth Apps must use <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/other-authentication-methods#basic-authentication">basic authentication</a> with their client ID and client secret to access this endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /marketplace_listing/plans/{plan_id}/accounts</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-accounts-for-a-plan--parameters"> <a href="#list-accounts-for-a-plan--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>plan_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>plan_id parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>sort</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>One of <code>created</code> (when the repository was starred) or <code>updated</code> (when it was last pushed to).</p> Default: <code>created</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>direction</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>To return the oldest accounts first, set to <code>asc</code>. Can be one of <code>asc</code> or <code>desc</code>. Ignored without the <code>sort</code> parameter.</p> </td> 
           </tr>

            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td>

           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Page number of the results to fetch.</p> Default: <code>1</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="get-a-subscription-plan-for-an-account-stubbed" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-a-subscription-plan-for-an-account-stubbed">Get a subscription plan for an account (stubbed)</a> </h3> 
         <p>Shows whether the user or organization account actively subscribes to a plan listed by the authenticated GitHub App. When someone submits a plan change that won't be processed until the end of their billing cycle, you will also see the upcoming pending change.</p> 
         <p>GitHub Apps must use a <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-a-github-app">JWT</a> to access this endpoint. OAuth Apps must use <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/other-authentication-methods#basic-authentication">basic authentication</a> with their client ID and client secret to access this endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /marketplace_listing/stubbed/accounts/{account_id}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="get-a-subscription-plan-for-an-account-stubbed--parameters"> <a href="#get-a-subscription-plan-for-an-account-stubbed--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4>

         <h3 id="list-plans-stubbed" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-plans-stubbed">List plans (stubbed)</a> </h3> 
         <p>Lists all plans that are part of your GitHub Marketplace listing.</p> 
         <p>GitHub Apps must use a <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-a-github-app">JWT</a> to access this endpoint. OAuth Apps must use <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/other-authentication-methods#basic-authentication">basic authentication</a> with their client ID and client secret to access this endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /marketplace_listing/stubbed/plans</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-plans-stubbed--parameters"> <a href="#list-plans-stubbed--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4>

          -->
