        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-accounts-for-a-plan-stubbed" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-accounts-for-a-plan-stubbed">List accounts for a plan (stubbed)</a> </h3> 
         <p>Returns repository and organization accounts associated with the specified plan, including free plans. For per-seat pricing, you see the list of accounts that have purchased the plan, including the number of seats purchased. When someone submits a plan change that won't be processed until the end of their billing cycle, you will also see the upcoming pending change.</p> 
         <p>GitHub Apps must use a <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-a-github-app">JWT</a> to access this endpoint. OAuth Apps must use <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/other-authentication-methods#basic-authentication">basic authentication</a> with their client ID and client secret to access this endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /marketplace_listing/stubbed/plans/{plan_id}/accounts</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-accounts-for-a-plan-stubbed--parameters"> <a href="#list-accounts-for-a-plan-stubbed--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>plan_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>plan_id parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>sort</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>One of <code>created</code> (when the repository was starred) or <code>updated</code> (when it was last pushed to).</p> Default: <code>created</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>direction</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>To return the oldest accounts first, set to <code>asc</code>. Can be one of <code>asc</code> or <code>desc</code>. Ignored without the <code>sort</code> parameter.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Results per page (max 100).</p> Default: <code>30</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Page number of the results to fetch.</p> Default: <code>1</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

         <h3 id="list-subscriptions-for-the-authenticated-user" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-subscriptions-for-the-authenticated-user">List subscriptions for the authenticated user</a> </h3> 
         <p>Lists the active subscriptions for the authenticated user. You must use a <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/identifying-and-authorizing-users-for-github-apps/#identifying-users-on-your-site">user-to-server OAuth access token</a>, created for a user who has authorized your GitHub App, to access this endpoint. . OAuth Apps must authenticate using an <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/">OAuth token</a>.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /user/marketplace_purchases</code></pre> 
        <div>

       <h2 id="webhooks"><a href="#webhooks">Webhooks</a></h2> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="get-a-webhook-configuration-for-an-app" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-a-webhook-configuration-for-an-app">Get a webhook configuration for an app</a> </h3> 
         <p>Returns the webhook configuration for a GitHub App. For more information about configuring a webhook for your app, see "<a href="/en/developers/apps/creating-a-github-app">Creating a GitHub App</a>."</p> 
         <p>You must use a <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-a-github-app">JWT</a> to access this endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /app/hook/config</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="get-a-webhook-configuration-for-an-app--code-samples"> <a href="#get-a-webhook-configuration-for-an-app--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/app/hook/config</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'GET /app/hook/config'</span>)
</code></pre> 
         <h4>Response</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 200 OK</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block">
          <pre><code class="hljs language-json">{
  <span class="hljs-attr">"content_type"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"json"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"insecure_ssl"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"0"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"secret"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"********"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"url"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"https://example.com/webhook"</span>
}
</code></pre>
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="update-a-webhook-configuration-for-an-app" class="pt-3"> <a href="#update-a-webhook-configuration-for-an-app">Update a webhook configuration for an app</a> </h3> 
         <p>Updates the webhook configuration for a GitHub App. For more information about configuring a webhook for your app, see "<a href="/en/developers/apps/creating-a-github-app">Creating a GitHub App</a>."</p> 
         <p>You must use a <a href="https://docs.github.com/apps/building-github-apps/authenticating-with-github-apps/#authenticating-as-a-github-app">JWT</a> to access this endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">patch</span> /app/hook/config</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="update-a-webhook-configuration-for-an-app--parameters"> <a href="#update-a-webhook-configuration-for-an-app--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>url</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The URL to which the payloads will be delivered.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>content_type</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The media type used to serialize the payloads. Supported values include <code>json</code> and <code>form</code>. The default is <code>form</code>.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>secret</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>If provided, the <code>secret</code> will be used as the <code>key</code> to generate the HMAC hex digest value for <a href="https://docs.github.com/webhooks/event-payloads/#delivery-headers">delivery signature headers</a>.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>insecure_ssl</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string or number</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Determines whether the SSL certificate of the host for <code>url</code> will be verified when delivering payloads. Supported values include <code>0</code> (verification is performed) and <code>1</code> (verification is not performed). The default is <code>0</code>. <strong>We strongly recommend not setting this to <code>1</code> as you are subject to man-in-the-middle and other attacks.</strong></p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="update-a-webhook-configuration-for-an-app--code-samples"> <a href="#update-a-webhook-configuration-for-an-app--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X PATCH \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/app/hook/config \
  -d '{"url":"url"}'</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'PATCH /app/hook/config'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">url</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'url'</span>
})
</code></pre> 
         <h4>Response</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 200 OK</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block">
          <pre><code class="hljs language-json">{
  <span class="hljs-attr">"content_type"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"json"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"insecure_ssl"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"0"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"secret"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"********"</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">"url"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"https://example.com/webhook"</span>
}
</code></pre>
         </div> 
        </div>
